5<//Rating>
<Text>Auryn Thai is open (no dine-in) during COVID! We love Thai and this is the first place we have tried since arriving in the area.

This is family owned (according to the manager) so that the family Grandma could share her love of cooking with her community. They only employ family members (during COVID) to keep risk low.

The food is simple, simply prepared, and nearly perfection.  Amazing flavors, aromas that make you salivate, and a variety of spice levels from "I thought this was Thai food," to "Dear Lord, what have I done."

Lemongrass, basil and a host of fresh vegetables provide the base for each dish. Adding your protein is easy and every protein from tofu to pork is succulent and prepared to the best possible state to carry flavor and create an amazing bite.

We can't wait to go back for more of Grandma's homemade Thai food!</Text><UserId.>118307736420999135483<//UserId.>< Resp>

<Text>Arguably the best Thai food I've ever had, and by far the best Thai food in Marin County. The service is excellent and the family that owns it are wonderful. This place is truly a hidden gem.

My top three suggestions:
Pumpkin red curry with beef
Pad Thai with beef (or shrimp)
Tom Kha Gai (chicken coconut soup)

P.S. This is one of the only places I'm getting take out from during the pandemic - because I've seen how cautious they are (ex. masks, hand sanitizer etc.). I am legitimately eating pumpkin curry as I write this :)</Text>< userid>

Wow! Delicious pizza, potatos, and chicken! We had a hungry group after a few hours up at the soccer fields and this really hit the spot. We ordered the combo #2 which came with a xl pizza, pound of potato slices, and a while broasted chicken. We added another large pizza and pound of potatoes.
